Feng Shaoshan's Report After Returning from an Inspection Tour: Discussing Industry and Commerce in Various Nanyang Regions

Mr. Feng Shaoshan, dispatched by the Ministry of Industry and Commerce to inspect industry and commerce in Nanyang, including Malaya, Lolo, Burma, India, Java, the Philippines, and Annam, has returned to Shanghai. The other day, the Shanghai National Products Promotion Federation hosted a banquet to welcome Mr. Feng, during which he gave a detailed speech on his inspection experiences and the state of industry and commerce in various Nanyang regions. He offered many instructions on the path for Chinese people to strive for in the future. The following is a record of Mr. Feng's speech. Brothers and comrades,

I have been promoting national products for over twenty years. In the meantime, I co-founded the Shanghai Citizens National Products Promotion Association, hoping that the work could proceed consistently without interruption. The motivation for this action was the deep feeling that our country's economy was lagging behind, and to remedy this, it was necessary to start from many aspects, and developing overseas trade was also urgent. Last autumn, I was fortunate enough to be dispatched by the Ministry of Industry and Commerce to Nanyang, including Malaya, Lolo, Burma, India, Java, the Philippines, and Annam, to inspect industry. Thereupon, I also took on the mission of promoting national products and developing overseas trade to the overseas Chinese, who all expressed enthusiastic support and cooperation. Today, I originally intended to give a detailed report on the situation in various regions and the above-mentioned actions to everyone present. However, Mr. Lin Kanghou and Mr. Wang Zhixin are here, having just returned from an inspection tour of Lolo, and are more familiar with the current situation there. For other regions, I believe many of you present have also been there. Also, time is not abundant today, so I will briefly talk about two important regions, East and West India, Calcutta and Bombay, and Burma, which will be separated from the Indian government and directly under the British government on April 1st of next year (1937). (A) Calcutta was the capital of British India. Our country has a consulate general there, a Chinese newspaper (called the India News), a party headquarters, various guild halls, a middle school, a Boy Scout troop, and a railway connecting to Darjeeling, and then to Tibet. (Darjeeling is located on the southern slope of the Himalayas, originally Sikkim of our Tibet, and was ceded to Britain in 1835). East of Darjeeling,

there is a place called Kalimpong, which is the main road from India to Tibet. (This area originally belonged to Bhutan of our Tibet and was occupied by Britain in 1865.) In addition, the area can reach the nearby Himalayan foothills of Nepal, Bhutan, Sikkim (also known as Denzong) and three small countries. There are more than 4,000 overseas Chinese in the area, most of whom are engaged in making leather shoes. There were originally more than 300 shoe stores there, all run by our overseas Chinese. Because of religious and class relations, Indians regard shoe making as a lowly occupation and are unwilling to do it, which has invisibly become the exclusive domain of our overseas Chinese. However, in recent years, European merchants, seeing that India has a population of more than 360 million, although Indians are accustomed to walking barefoot as a courtesy and are located in the tropics, not all people need shoes, but the business is also considerable. Therefore,

recently, foreign businessmen have also been thinking about getting a share of the shoe business, which was previously monopolized by overseas Chinese, and have plans to covet the shoe market. They use machines to make shoes, which produce the most. In particular, the Czech Bata company, relying on its strong capital, first established a branch in the area to promote its products, to defeat the shoe stores run by overseas Chinese and seek to monopolize the market. They recruited young Indian children to study in the company. After obtaining considerable experience, they were sent to the Czech Republic for field research. After returning to India, they were given loans to open branches everywhere, selling at low prices. The shoe business of overseas Chinese has been greatly affected. Recently, only more than 200 shoe stores remain, and their future is not optimistic. When I was there, I investigated the shoe stores run by overseas Chinese. The reason why they cannot compete with foreign businessmen and gradually lose money is not entirely due to

foreign businessmen dumping, but also because not only can colleagues not unite, but they also compete with each other, which is also a major factor in self-destruction. Therefore, I gave the local overseas Chinese merchants advice, hoping that they could contact each other and form a public guild. All products from each store must first be sent to the public guild, and the selling price should be determined according to the quality and grade, so as not to reduce prices and compete with each other and be wiped out by foreign merchants. In Calcutta, in addition to the above-mentioned leather shoe industry, which is monopolized by people from Meixian, Guangdong, there are also people from Taishan and Kaiping in Guangdong, who are engaged in the timber industry, as carpenters, and opening grocery stores, porcelain shops, and bars (bars are businesses that operate in wine. They must vote to the government every year, and those who pay the highest amount are allowed to open), and other businesses, but most of them are located in Chinatown. In addition, there are people from Shandong who sell Shandong silk, lace produced in Chaozhou and Shantou in Guangdong, etc. Although the number of overseas Chinese in Calcutta and the industries they engage in cannot be said to be small, the Chinese Chamber of Commerce has not yet been organized. The reason is that factions are divided, and it is not easy to unite, which is a common shortcoming of our people. However, in the near future, I hope it will be achieved, because when I was there, I had several discussions with enthusiastic overseas Chinese leaders in the area. They all believe that it is urgent to organize. When I was there, the lace merchants among our overseas Chinese, after my persuasion, immediately organized the Preparatory Committee of the Calcutta Lace Industry Association. By analogy, the Calcutta Chinese Chamber of Commerce will soon be established and will seek welfare for our overseas Chinese. (B) Bombay is an important commercial port in Western India. Its commerce can reach the Kashgar province of India (on the border of Xinjiang in our country) and Balochistan, Afghanistan.

Persia and other countries. Our country has a vice consulate, party headquarters, schools, and other institutions there. The population of the area is 1,157,851, slightly less than the 1,419,321 in Calcutta, the city of East India, but it is the second most populous city in India. There are more than 1,000 overseas Chinese there, most of whom are from Taishan and Kaiping in Guangdong. Chinatown also has grocery stores and restaurants. In the Indian Muslim Quarter, there are overseas Chinese who specialize in silk and groceries from Guangdong, with an annual turnover of 3 million yuan (Indian Rupees). They have also organized a commercial and sports club. In recent years, because business in India has improved compared to before, hundreds of people from Shandong have been returning to the port one after another. Most of them take ships directly from Shanghai to their business locations and specialize in Shandong silk and Chaozhou and Shantou lace and fine cloth from Guangdong. The people of Lu are strong and able to endure hardships. They carry large packages on their backs every day and sell them in the inland villages by bicycle. Bombay now has the Shandong Fellow Association. The chairman and vice chairman who preside over the association are very good people. When they hosted banquets to welcome me and when the overseas Chinese compatriots held a general assembly to welcome me, I tried my best to encourage them to love the country and the community, especially the fellow association, which should hold a meeting one day of each week, to advise everyone to do the duty of a great nation and not to show any shortcomings that would be despised by other countries. Moreover, when doing business in the interior, they should be familiar with the commercial situation, pay attention to courtesy, and sell genuine products at fair prices. They agreed with me very much. (C) Burma is bordered by Siam to the east, the Bay of Bengal to the south, and the province of Assam in India to the west. (To be continued)

Labor Dispute at Hongxing Hosiery Factory: Mediation Again: Principles Submitted to Director for Review

The Hongxing Hosiery Factory on Caishi Road in the French Concession experienced a labor dispute due to a conflict between employees and female workers. Although the party and government agencies persuaded them to make a four-point decision, the factory was deeply afraid of further disputes and has not implemented it. To eliminate the dispute, the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau summoned both parties to the bureau again yesterday afternoon at 2 pm to formally implement mediation. Li Weixiong from the Municipal Party Department, Wang Shui (represented by Zhang Chuqiang) from the Social Affairs Bureau, Ge Suisheng and Le Shunting representing the capitalists, Zhang Zhuyun from the Second District Knitting Industry Union representing the labor, and Zhi Weixin from the factory's union branch were present. After both parties stated their opinions, the labor demanded that the factory follow the four principles set by the Social Affairs Bureau. The capitalists could not agree to this from beginning to end, so the mediation still yielded no results. Then the chairman of the committee said that these principles would be determined after the director has reviewed and approved them.

Tobacco and Grocery Industry Demands Supplementary Bonuses for Gu Ben Soap: Based on Wholesale Practices, Each Six Pieces to be Replenished

Since the launch of Gu Ben Soap, self-made by the Wuzhou Pharmacy in this city, patriots have been eagerly promoting it. However, the most capable promoters are the tobacco and grocery stores. Recently, the Family Invincible Soap, Xiangmao Soap, and Mi Soap have emerged to compete, but the sales of each soap are still the highest for Gu Ben Soap. Because the shareholders of the Dacheng Company, the manager of the soap, have very good relations with various tobacco and grocery stores, they are all willing to promote sales and sacrifice prices. They also contact various tobacco companies to replace gifts with Gu Ben Soap when exchanging empty shells. Therefore, the number of sales is increasing day by day. It is now learned that Xiangmao Bai Mi Soap has added investigators to investigate the procedures of the industry in the city. The procedure has been completed, and samples of soap and advertisements have been distributed door-to-door, encouraging the stores to promote sales in a unified manner. For every ten boxes sold, one box is added as a gift. In addition to promoting and displaying the soap in major companies, tobacco and grocery stores also account for seven tenths of the sales. However, the Dacheng Company, which manages Gu Ben Soap, has only supplemented six Gu Ben Soaps per box at the old price for large wholesale companies since August. No supplements are given to small companies. The small companies believe that the Dacheng Company's treatment is unfair, and they have repeatedly sent people to the company to request a supplementary gift of soap, but they have been rejected. Later, after Shen Weiting, chairman of the Tobacco and Grocery Industry Association, and committee members Qiu Tanglin, Mi Chuxin, and Chen Kunxian, negotiated with the company again, there were still no results. The stores in the industry are now writing letters to the association one after another, continuing to ask the chairman and committee members to request a supplementary gift from the company to maintain their business.

Smuggling Morphine into the US Case: Associate in Shanghai: French National Stai Commits Suicide: Massive Overdose of Narcotics, Resuscitation Ineffective, Dies: No Explanation of Morphine Case Inside Story

Stai, the Chief Accountant of the Baolong Hospital in this port, who was related to the case of Ms. Wen Mali privately transporting morphine into the United States, was fired by the hospital director after the case was revealed, and then declared missing. Although the three police authorities in this port issued arrest warrants, they were not successful. Now, he has also died, following the suicide of Mr. Branderstetter, the leader of the private drug trafficking ring. At 7:30 the night before last night, a Chinese person passing through a field somewhere on Xujiahui Road saw a foreigner lying under a tree. Although he temporarily regained consciousness before his death, he was unable to explain anything about the private smuggling of morphine by Ms. Wen Mali. Stai was 50 years old and was from Alsace, France. He must have committed suicide out of fear of crime in his hiding place the night before last night and was found lying under a tree after taking the drug. It is said that a French passport was found in his pocket, as well as ten dollars in paper money. Whether there are other exhibits, the people in the police station do not want to reveal it now, because they believe that there are other leaders of the private drug trafficking ring hiding in Shanghai and plan to arrest them, fearing that the news will leak and cause inconvenience. Although Stai lived in Shanghai for about 20 years and had a small house, he usually lived in seclusion and had no friends. French overseas Chinese in this port did not know him. Even the French Consular Office and the police station did not know him. He served in the Binlong Hospital, lived in a small room, and did not go out easily, so he was very trusted by the director. It was unexpected that he would be the leader of a private drug trafficking ring. Now his body is still stopped at the autopsy place, and it is heard that an autopsy will be performed to see what kind of drug he took to die.

Failed to Buy an Official Position: Allegations of Collusion and Fraud: Blocked from Taking Office Twice: Security Deposit of Several Hundred Dollars Lost

Jiang Gongding and Ding Huian, (resident at No. 10 Mao Yili, Meimen Road, Shanhai Pass) from Changzhou, were previously deceived of their security deposits for seeking the position of Chief of the Tobacco and Liquor License Tax Inspection Office in Chuansha County. They sued Cao Shanxiang, former director (resident at No. 5, Lane 141, Dasheng Hutong, Haig Road), Li Shiyuan, director's wife, Wang Zhiliang, incumbent director (resident at No. 30 Yuzhen Lane, Malang Road), and Gao Ruirong (resident at No. 3 Junyili, Er'jin Road) for collusion and fraud in the Criminal Division of the Second Special Court. It was alleged that in February of this year, through the introduction of his friend Ding Huian, he met Gao Ruirong. According to Gao, his friend Cao Shanxiang was the Chief of the Tobacco and Liquor License Tax Bureau of Shangdou, Taijia, Chuan, and other counties. If he wanted to seek the position of Chief in Chuansha, he only needed a security deposit of several hundred yuan to succeed. At that time, Ding was idle, so they jointly raised 900 yuan, stating that the position of Chief would be handled by Ding Huian and Gao Ruirong. After the procedures were completed, Ding and Gao took the money to the bureau for negotiation the next day. Director Cao Shanxiang was out on business, so Director's wife Li Shiyuan accompanied them to the First District Tobacco and Liquor License Tax Bureau on Fusantang Street, Nanshi. Li Shiyuan ordered Ding and Gao to hand over the money to her, and the bureau issued a receipt, instructing them to go to the bureau on the 13th to collect the appointment letter. When the time came, they obtained documents such as stamped official documents and went to the Chuansha County Government. The head of Jin Section met them and explained that the director had been replaced, and Cao Shanxiang had been dismissed and replaced by Wang Zhiliang as the director. Later, after repeated negotiations with the new director, Wang Zhiliang, the incumbent director, agreed to seek a job for him, but he had to add a security deposit. At that time, he paid 200 yuan in cash and a promissory note for 450 yuan. After completing the procedures, he went to Chuansha again to take over the job. The head of Jin Section of the County Government said that the bureau had been ordered by the Department of Finance to be merged into the Business Tax Bureau, etc. The defendants' behavior was clearly collusion and fraud, requesting that they be interrogated and dealt with according to law. The court accepted the lawsuit and issued summonses several times. Because the first defendant Cao Shanxiang lived in Nanjing and the summons could not be delivered, the court requested the Capital Court to arrest Cao and transfer him to the Second Special Court. Yesterday morning, presiding Judge Zhang Minsheng interrogated him in the Second Criminal Court. Because the other defendants had not been summoned, only Cao Shanxiang was questioned. He claimed that the security deposit was not handled by him, and he gave evasive answers. The court adjourned the hearing and summoned the defendants to appear in court for further interrogation.

Shanghai Tram Company Bans Vending on Trams to Avoid Disturbing Public Order

General factories and businesses in Shanghai employ salespersons to promote their products and sell their goods along various roads or on trams to boost sales. Recently, the practice has become widespread, resulting in vendors peddling various goods on every tram at all times. It is reported that the Shanghai Tram Company, considering this sales behavior a disruption of public passenger order, has immediately issued a ban and has painted a warning in white paint on the trams stating, "No goods of any kind are allowed to be sold on the tram." Consequently, the number of vendors selling goods on trams has decreased in recent days.

National Touring Troupe Arrives in Shanghai, Expanding Solicitation of Sponsorship

The New Safety National Touring Troupe, which departed from Huai'an last autumn and passed through Zhenjiang, Nanjing, Pukou, Bengbu, Wuhu, Anqing, and other places, has recently arrived in Shanghai under the leadership of Mr. Zai Dazhi and is temporarily residing at Yuying Elementary School on Route Cardinal Mercier. Yesterday, a rural society reporter visited the leader and received the following statement: "Our troupe is organized by a dozen or so young people around the age of fifteen. The purpose is to make society our school. Since our departure on National Day last year, we have spent ten months passing through more than a dozen cities and towns, encountering various difficulties, but we have overcome them all. Our goal is to learn and forge strong character while focusing on how to help those people who have fewer opportunities to receive knowledge than we do. The national crisis is serious. Mr. Sun Yat-sen said, 'We must awaken the masses.' Facts tell us that this work is very important. This time, we have come to Shanghai to learn essential knowledge and skills during the summer vacation while organizing everything from the past and discussing future plans in detail. Therefore, there is a need to expand our plan. We have decided that our subsequent itinerary will take us through Zhejiang, Anhui, Jiangxi, Hunan, Hubei, and other provinces with developed highways. Therefore, there is a need to prepare our own large automobile. This large automobile will be our school and the school for the people in the places we pass through. Automobiles are modern means of transportation. We must acquire driving knowledge and skills. We must first acquire the tools. This is beyond doubt. We will make our best effort to achieve our goals. To make our work more effective during the trip, we deeply feel the pain of having insufficient or unsuitable tools. The total value of the required books, tools, and supplies is about four or five thousand yuan, which is a very large sum. How can we manage to do it? However, the ancient saying goes, 'Many little bits make a coat, and many hands make light work.' To hope for the success of our plan, we can only make our request, collect widespread sponsorship, and think that the elders and young friends who are enthusiastic about us creating new lives will surely give us great strength in sponsorship and guidance. Regarding the methods of soliciting sponsorship, there are: (1) Sponsoring with materials, such as a three-ton automobile, a 16mm projector, a 16mm movie camera, and a five-power telescope, etc.; (2) Sponsoring with cash, regardless of the amount; (3) Exchanging with advertisements, such as factories, shops, or cultural and academic institutions, entrusting with advertisements or properly arranging for inland work to exchange for materials or cash. It is heard that they will set off at the beginning of next month, first to Hangzhou, and then to Anhui, Jiangxi, and other places for travel."

Abortion Due to Impending Marriage Leads to Tragic Death: Wang Lanying Regrets Her Actions; Wang Long's Family Released on Bail Pending Trial

Wang Lanying, a twenty-year-old woman from Anhui who worked at the Tongxing Yarn Factory on Route Woosung, was betrothed by her parents to someone from a young age. Unexpectedly, the woman had an affair in Shanghai with a fellow villager named Chen, and after several encounters, she became pregnant. Now, her husband's family has selected an auspicious date to welcome her into the family. Her mother, Wang Long, came to Shanghai to bring her daughter back to her hometown so the marriage could take place. But with the date fast approaching, there was no way to get rid of the fetus in her womb. On the 12th of this month, the mother and daughter went to room number 18 of the Yong'an Hotel on Route Shuntak. The daughter went to a certain place on Yangtszepoo Road and hired a midwife surnamed Li to perform an abortion, agreeing on a fee of fourteen yuan. At 7 PM that evening, Ms. Li went to the hotel and performed the procedure, using a bamboo chopstick to insert it into the woman's vagina. By the 15th, the mother saw that her daughter's condition had worsened, so she accompanied her to the Huxi Hospital at 115 Route Maignan. The doctor diagnosed that it was caused by an abortion and reported it to the Zhabei Police Station. Detective Wang Qishan was ordered to investigate. The woman was transferred to Guangren Hospital for treatment. Although the fetus was aborted, the woman's condition worsened and she died at 2:25 PM on the 20th. The detectives suspected Wang Long's family of assisting in the abortion and took her to the police station for custody. The midwife had fled upon hearing the news, so there was no way to arrest her. Yesterday morning, Ms. Wang was sent to the First Special Court. Judge Huang Risheng held a hearing and ordered a postponement for further investigation. Ms. Wang was released on bail to be available for questioning. Around 10 AM, prosecutor Zhang Zongru, accompanied by medical examiners Wei and Zhang, and clerk Wang Zuyi, went to the morgue on Route Frelon to examine the body. After examination, it was determined that the deceased Wang Lanying, female, had died due to illness caused by an abortion during her lifetime. The body was temporarily entrusted to Puji Villa for embalming, pending the release of her mother, Wang Long, on bail.

Liu Huizhi and Others Accused of Embezzlement; Trial Begins; "Flying Over the Sea" Gains Over 20,000 Taels of Gold; Over 10 Million in Transactions with "Hengji Account"

Liu Huizhi, the current managing director and former manager of the China Industrial Bank, and Li Jizhi, were criminally prosecuted by the bank's shareholders Zhang Chongfu, He Jiechun, and others to the First Special District Court for allegedly embezzling and defrauding the bank of millions of dollars. Because the plaintiffs' claims in both cases were largely the same, the court decided to consolidate the cases for trial. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Chuan Lin held a hearing. He first stated that the handling judge had been transferred, so the case must be re-examined. The plaintiff's lawyer, Chen Tan, then presented the indictment, first detailing the content of the accusation of fraudulently raising the stock price of the Beijing Waterworks Company. He stated that the stock was purchased for a price of more than 33,800 yuan. The defendant then suddenly raised the price to more than 50,200 yuan, paying one side to the account of the China Industrial Bank and collecting the other side to the account of Gongshunji. Although the defendant claimed that the name Gongshunji was the incarnation of the bank, the plaintiff knew that it was the defendant's alias. The defendant only spent a moment transferring the account and embezzled more than 20,000 taels of bank funds. This kind of fraudulent method is called "flying over the sea" in accounting terms. After this procedure, even money can fly into the pocket. In court, the defendant Liu Huizhi was asked how he defended this accusation. Liu stated that the name of the Gongshunji account had been approved by the board of directors, and the accounts recorded therein were confidential and could not be disclosed to outsiders. The stock price was raised because there was hope of selling it at the time. Although it was not sold later, I have repeatedly transferred the account to prevent the bank from suffering losses. Lawyer Chen then recounted the accusation of fraudulently establishing the Hengji account name to embezzle. He stated that the defendant initially denied this.

The name of the Hengji account, and it was not until the plaintiff investigated and found that Hengji was affiliated with the Hengshun Trust Company founded by the defendant, and presented various evidence, that he claimed that Hengji was the account name of Jia Yangshan. In fact, the Hengshun Company was run by the defendant, and Hengji was not the account of Jia Yangshan. The previous record of the Hengshun Company's resolution, which was retrieved, contains the record that Liu Huizhi once represented Hengji to attend the shareholders' meeting. However, the loopholes in this resolution record are obvious. The most obvious ones are: (1) The color of the thread used to bind the book is clearly different in newness from the color of the cover. (2) The Qingyunge Bookstore, which sold the Chu book, has a red stamp with fifty pages on the back, but when counted, there are only forty pages, and ten pages have been torn off. (3) There are still remnants left where it was torn. All these points should be given extra attention. In addition, the shareholder register and shareholder general ledger of Hengshun Company do not have the name of Liu Huizhi, but Liu has already admitted that he is a shareholder of Hengshun and has paid 10,000 yuan for the shares. Under what name did he subscribe for the shares? It should be investigated. Hengji was the account that received cash from the China Industrial Bank that year, receiving 40,000 yuan every day and using 14.4 million yuan every year. With such a huge amount of transactions, how could the defendant not know who Hengji was? This point needs to be thoroughly investigated. Judge Chuan then stated that the case was complicated and that the evidence that needed to be investigated was very numerous. He then postponed the trial to another date.

Route 17 Trolleybuses Will Extend to New Routes; Service Expected to Begin Mid-Next Month

Route 17 trolleybuses, which run north-south through the British and French concessions, originally ran from Route Kunming in the British Concession to Route Zikawei in the French Concession. The route will now be extended to Dapu Bridge at the end of Route Père Robert. After the service begins, the bus will turn from Route Tsai Shi into Route Conty, pass through Route Siccawei, and go to Dapu Bridge on Route Père Robert. However, this will not affect traffic on Route Zikawei because the Route 18 bus terminates there. This extended route is not very long and will significantly shorten the distance between the Central District and the southwest area of the French Concession. The power lines are currently being laid, and service is expected to begin in mid-next month.

Wife Unfaithful, Contract Signed for Sale; Paramour Unable to Pay Flees; Servant's Criminal Complaint Dismissed

Xu Yandi, a servant residing at 91 Route Tenant de la Tour, French Concession, is over thirty years old. His wife, Jiang, named Azong, is about the same age. They have a son and a daughter, the daughter is twelve years old this year, and the son is five years old. Unexpectedly, Xu's wife, Jiang, was restless and had an affair with Weng Shaocong, a colleague residing at 33 Route de Zikawei near Xu's house. They had been secretly having an affair for some time. After Xu discovered the adultery, Xu and his wife, Jiang, agreed to divorce. The two parties signed a written agreement, agreeing that the two children would be led and raised by Xu. On one side, Jiang was sold to Weng Shaocong as his wife, and Weng compensated Xu for the loss. The two parties signed another contract. Because Weng was unable to pay the money for a while, he signed another document and gave it to Xu for safekeeping. Later, Weng and Jiang Azong lived together. They were still unable to pay Xu's losses and repeatedly delayed the payment. Recently, they fled together. Xu then hired a lawyer to file a complaint with the Criminal Court of the Second Special Court, accusing Jiang Azong and Weng Shaocong of interfering with marriage, requesting investigation, and attaching a civil complaint to seek compensation for the loss. The court, according to the complaint, held a hearing yesterday by Judge Chen Shuoying. The two defendants were unable to be summoned and did not arrive. Only the plaintiff, Xu Yandi, and his lawyer arrived and recounted the previous requests. The court verified the words and stated that since the two parties had signed a contract, they should file a lawsuit with the civil court, which did not involve criminal matters. The court then announced that Jiang Azong and Weng Shaocong were not guilty.

Shoe-Shining Service Group's Work Progressing Smoothly; Shoe-Shining Revenue for the First Eight Months of This Year is Considerable, Totalling Over 1,000 Yuan

Working Condition

When the group was established last year, there were a total of twelve service members, all of whom were trained by the former general secretary, Ye Fanggui, and then sent to various barber shops, hotels, and amusement parks, such as Dagongming Barber Shop, Datong Hotel, and Tianyunlou, to provide services. Because the service members have the sympathy of people from all walks of life, their work is also very convenient. Recently, Mr. Zhang resigned due to certain reasons, and the group affairs will be presided over by someone appointed by the executive committee.

Shoe-Shining Revenue

Regarding the work results from January to August of this year, the group reported the following yesterday. The total income from the work in the first eight months of this year was 1,156 yuan and 12 cents. The month with the highest income was April, with 188 yuan and 80 cents. The month with the lowest income was January, with 86 yuan and 33 cents. Yang Yinhai, Conning with Fake Diamond Ring; Pawnshop Employee Already Deceived Once; Unexpectedly, Yang Scams Again

Yang Yinhai, a 29-year-old man from Zhenjiang residing at 4 Daokaw Lane Street, Nanshi, Huajie, has been dealing in Western-style jewelry. On the evening of the 18th of this month, he held a Western-style imitation diamond ring and asked the Guanglifeng pawnshop at No. 235 Xizilaihuo Street, at the corner of Route Tsai Shi, French Concession, for 80 yuan. The pawnshop employee, Shen Changnian (32 years old, local), looked at it under the light and saw that the diamond was beautifully polished, estimating that its value was in the hundreds of gold. He did not realize that it was a fake, so he pawned it for the amount. After closing the market, he matched the goods and found out that he had been deceived and could not pursue the matter. He could only regret his bad luck and compensate the store for the principal. Unexpectedly, Yang was not satisfied and on the evening of the 20th, he held another similar fake diamond ring, slightly larger than the previous one, and still went to the pawnshop to ask for 150 yuan. Pawnshop employee Shen Changnian pretended to deal with him and secretly sent an apprentice out the back door to report to the French police station. Detectives rushed to the scene and took Yang and the two fake diamond rings into the police station. It was found that the fake diamonds were made of Japanese zircons, and they were indistinguishable from real diamonds under the light. After interrogation by the police chief, Yang was taken into custody. Yesterday, he was sent to the Criminal Court 8 of the Second Special Court for interrogation by Judge Sun Penghuan.

The Police Department's lawyer, Chen Ming, explained the case and requested a postponement of the investigation to determine whether the defendant had committed other crimes, so that they could be prosecuted together. The investigating officer presented the fake diamond ring to the court. The plaintiff, Shen Changnian, then explained the situation of the defendant mixing fake diamond rings twice. The court verified the report and interrogated the defendant. Then, it was ordered to postpone the investigation to the 24th and detain the defendant.

Cattle Plague Found in This City; Milk Production Greatly Reduced; All Parties Currently Working Hard to Eradicate

According to the Industry Association, cattle plague has recently occurred in this city. Since the disease occurred, milk production has decreased slightly, but it has no effect on nutrition and cleanliness. It is heard that after the disease was discovered, all parties have been working hard to eradicate it, so the disease has gradually decreased in recent days.

True Self-Disciplined Buddhist Monk

Master Puqin, originally from Rongchang County, Sichuan Province, with the surname Pan, came from a charitable family. When the Master was young, he wanted to become a monk and practice, but his parents did not allow it. He secretly escaped to Leixi Temple on Mount Emei and took the Venerable Daming as his teacher. As soon as he became a monk, he thought of ending his life and escaping death, and did not learn chanting, but specialized in practicing, widely speaking Buddhist scriptures and studying Buddhism. He previously pricked his tongue and wrote the Lotus Sutra, the Diamond Sutra, the Amitabha Sutra, and other scriptures in Chengdu, countless times. He went south to Putuo to worship the pagoda by burning his fingers at Yuzhou Temple and writing two parts of the Lotus Sutra in blood for twenty-three years. He was taught secret teachings by Venerable Rongzeng of the Bodhi Society. Later, he wrote the Avatamsaka Sutra in blood in seclusion at the Haihui Zen Temple with the Venerable Ci Fa, and forgot to speak for a year, specializing in Esoteric Buddhism. He also burned forty-eight lamps on his body and mind. One of the lamps was as large as a teacup mouth. He spent the whole night sacrificing his life to the Buddha and managed to escape the danger. The lamp marks gradually healed. On June 19th of this year, he made offerings to the Buddha and burned twelve lamps on both sides of his back, and wrote the Avatamsaka Sutra in his tongue blood. Every morning, he bled half a cup, and wrote from 6:00 AM to 4:00 PM without feeling bitter. His tongue was not damaged, and his spirit was as usual. On July 15th, he held a large lamp-burning ceremony, making offerings to the Buddha and the monks, benefiting people and gods, and praying for world peace. He felt the diligence of the monks and laity, and more than 30 disciples who converted to the Buddha burned lamps and incense. He is a true ascetic monk of Buddhism.

Sun Shengtang, a Ningbo native residing at No. 1, Jishen Lane, Kangding Road, Shanghai West, whose son, Sun Yushu, is a bus ticket seller, recently hired lawyer Qu Shiji to file a lawsuit in the local court, accusing his son's colleague, Zhang Amao, of coercing a written agreement and fraudulently obtaining money. Yesterday, Judge Lu Hongyi opened the court session. Sun Shengtang testified that he is 52 years old. On the 15th of this month, at 10 AM, the defendant, Zhang Amao, brought a policeman from the Caojiadu Public Security Bureau to the plaintiff's home and arrested his son, Yushu, claiming that Zhang Amao's wife, Zhang Liu, had committed adultery with Yushu, and that Zhang Amao had reported it, hence the arrest. Finally, Zhang Amao, along with several others, rebuked him and prevented him from leaving, stating that in the case of Sun Yushu's adultery with his wife, they had hired lawyer Ye Foukang, costing 300 yuan, which should be compensated. Otherwise, he would not let the father and son return home, and ordered his accomplices to guard the exit. Faced with this precarious situation, and being outnumbered and intimidated, he was persuaded by accomplices to mediate. He was forced to write an agreement for 220 yuan, which Zhang Amao took before he was released. Therefore, he requested legal action. The defendant, Zhang Amao, testified that he is 29 years old, a Ningbo native residing at No. 439 Kangding Road. Sun Yushu and he lived in the same room and were formerly colleagues. He discovered that Yushu had an affair with his wife, and on the 12th of this month, he reported the situation to the Caojiadu branch bureau. On the 15th of the same month, the police bureau ordered the police to arrest Sun Yushu. After interrogation, Sun Yushu's father and friend Jiang Mingdong and others repeatedly persuaded him to reconcile at the branch bureau and agreed to compensate him for the 220 yuan in lawyer's fees, and a written agreement was made. He requested investigation, stating that there was no coercion or fraudulent acquisition of money. At this point, lawyer Qu stated that since the defendant had hired a lawyer, he requested that the lawyer be summoned to court for cross-examination. The court ruled that the case should be investigated further after summoning lawyer Ye as a witness.

The publication has 34 issues per year, priced at one yuan. All post offices nationwide can subscribe on behalf of the publisher.

Highway "Wooden Bridge" Published. The China National Road Construction Association has compiled and printed more than a dozen road and municipal administration series books over the years. Recently, because there is still a lack of special books on the construction of wooden bridges in China, it has specially invited civil engineering expert Zhao Guohua to compile the book "Wooden Bridge" to meet the needs of the times. The content of the book is extremely rich. Whether it is the design and construction of wooden bridges for rural highways and railways, all are discussed in detail. Every sentence and formula has been carefully considered and calculated by the author, making it a good reference book for bridge construction in China. The entire book has more than 300 pages, with more than 100,000 words, more than 120 illustrations, and 33 attached tables, printed on high-quality paper and bound in a thick hardcover volume. It is now published and sold for 2 yuan in national currency. The distributor is No. 70 Gubalu Road, Shanghai.

Medical Field

Zhou Jifu Cures Rare and Difficult Diseases. Dr. Zhou Jifu in this city is a graduate of a Western medical school, specializing in internal and surgical medicine, especially good at opium withdrawal. He has been practicing medicine in Shanghai for more than ten years. With his extensive knowledge, superb skills, and rich experience, all those who seek treatment from him are brought back to life. Recently, General Wu Zuojun, a well-known figure in the Shandong military, suffered from a fistula with pus and tubes several inches long, which had not been cured by many doctors. After Dr. Zhou treated him, he performed a minor operation and completely cured him in a few weeks. In addition, Wang Boxin suffered from neurasthenia, a disease that is not easy to treat. Recently, after Dr. Zhou diagnosed and treated him, the medicine cured the disease in just three days, and he recovered his health. He can be called a miracle doctor. It is said that Dr. Zhou provides consultation every morning at No. 152 Haining Road, telephone 45348, and in the afternoon he provides consultation at the Nanyang Pharmacy on Nanjing Road.

Letters to the Editor

Dear Editor, in your newspaper's 5th edition on September 20th, there was a news story about our bank employee Xu Longyuan embezzling 6,000 yuan. Mr. Xu was dismissed at the end of last year. For the sake of clarification, we are writing to request a correction. We would be very grateful. Sincerely, The Da Kang Bank.

Dear Editor, Upon reading the local news in your newspaper on September 21st, there was an article about the Fresh Pork Industry Association convening a meeting to rectify industry regulations. We were very surprised. Our association has not convened any meetings with members to discuss this issue. The news published by your newspaper must be based on inaccurate reporting. We are writing to request that you investigate and promptly make a correction. Thank you very much. Secretariat of the Shanghai Fresh Pork Industry Association, September 21st.

Weather Report

The Xujiahui Observatory's weather forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday stated that Shandong is sunny to partly cloudy, with southwest to northwest winds. The Yellow River basin and the upper and middle reaches of the Yangtze River have southwest to southeast breezes. The lower reaches of the Yangtze River have southeast to southwest winds and morning fog. The East China Sea and Taiwan are cloudy to overcast with northeast winds. Also, the highest temperature in this city within the 24 hours before 3 PM yesterday was 89.6 degrees, and the lowest was 50.4 degrees. On the same day last year, the highest was 80.1 degrees, and the lowest was 62.1 degrees.

Sports News

World Games Delegation to Arrive in Shanghai Soon; Various Circles in the City Prepare to Welcome Them; Preparatory Committee Established at Yesterday's City Government Meeting

The Chinese delegation to the World Games departed from Europe on the 4th of this month and is returning home. They were originally scheduled to arrive in Shanghai on the 27th of this month, but the Contelossa ship's engines were damaged in Pompeii, delaying the voyage and pushing their arrival to the 3rd of next month. Various circles in the city, recognizing that the delegation's trip abroad, although not victorious in terms of skill, has left a deep impression on people around the world, held a meeting at 2 PM yesterday in the first conference room of the municipal government to discuss welcoming arrangements upon their arrival. Details are as follows:

Attendees

Those present at yesterday's preparatory meeting included City Government Secretary Zhang Tingrong, Section Chief Li Dachao, City Education Bureau Section Chiefs Jiang Jianbai and Wang Keyong, City Sports Field Acting Director Wang Fudan, Director Li Jiyuan, Huang Yanpei of the China Vocational Education Society, Xu Zexiang of the People's Education Center, Ling Xitao of the YMCA, Lu Lihua of the Liangjiang Women's Physical Education School, and representatives from various organizations, more than twenty people in total. Li Dachao was elected as chairman.

Establishment of the Preparatory Committee

Resolutions: (1) Establish a preparatory committee for welcoming the World Games delegation's return to the country today (temporarily located in the First Section of the City Government) to prepare for large-scale welcome activities; (2) The welcome activities are divided into (A) gathering at the pier to welcome the Contelossa ship upon its arrival, and (B) holding a grand welcome reception at the YMCA in the Eight Immortals Bridge.

Pier Welcome

(3) Regarding item (A), those going to the pier to welcome the delegation include (1) all participating organizations must each send four representatives, and letters will be sent to the Boy Scout Association, the Municipal Physical Education School, and relevant schools to line up and welcome them at the pier; (2) a special ship will be prepared to sail to the outer Wusongkou to welcome them, and each organization is only allowed to send one responsible representative to participate, and must notify the preparatory committee of the list in advance to calculate the cabin space. The remaining representatives and organizations are only allowed to line up and welcome them at the pier; (3) flags and firecrackers will be prepared to be set off at the dock at that time; (4) a letter will be sent to the Aviation Association to send two airplanes to fly to the outer Wusongkou to welcome and escort the Contelossa ship into port; (5) two girls will present flowers (candidates are still being sought).

Welcome Reception

(4) Regarding the welcome reception in item (B), the following measures are to be taken: (1) Time: The time for the welcome reception is tentatively scheduled for the afternoon of the same day at the YMCA in the Eight Immortals Bridge. If the Contelossa ship arrives in Shanghai in the afternoon, it will be postponed until the next day; (2) each participating organization may send two representatives to participate; (5) welcome badges are divided into two types: one for representatives of participating organizations and welcome personnel to wear, and one for the welcomees to wear for identification; (6) other matters will be scheduled for the next preparatory meeting as necessary, and it is hoped that all participating organizations and welcome personnel will attend on time.

World Games Athlete Delegation Accompanying Records, 14th Letter

— Special Correspondent Feng Youzhen from Central News Agency

(63) Day 10 of the Games

On the 10th day of the Games, the athletics competition has completely ended, and the atmosphere in the main venue has become deserted. The swimming pool, however, has become the focus of the audience's interest. The schedule for the day is as follows:

7 AM: Calisthenics; 8 AM: Bicycle Race; 9 AM: Swimming and Fencing; 9:30 AM: Rowing; 2 PM: Calisthenics; 3 PM: Boxing, Swimming, and Fencing; 4 PM: Basketball, Football, and Handball; 4:30 PM: Hockey; 8 PM: Fencing; 8:30 PM: Boxing; 9 PM: Music and Dance Performances. The swimming results are recorded as follows:

Swimming

800-Meter Relay. The 800-meter relay was held at 10:30 AM, with 21 countries participating, divided into three preliminary rounds (the first and second rounds each had seven countries, and the third round had six countries, but Chile in the first round and Peru in the second round did not participate temporarily). The top two from each group and the two fastest third-place finishers from the three groups participated in the final. The Japanese team in the first group had the best result, with a time of only 8 minutes and 56.1 seconds, breaking the previous Games record of 8 minutes and 55.4 seconds set by Japan. The results of each group are as follows:

First Group

(1) France, 9 minutes 21 seconds

(2) Canada, 9 minutes 40 seconds

Second Group

(1) USA, 9 minutes 10.4 seconds

(2) Hungary, 9 minutes 20.8 seconds

Third Group

(1) Japan, 8 minutes 56.1 seconds (New Games Record)

(2) Germany, 9 minutes 21.4 seconds

Women's 100-Meter Freestyle Final. The women's 100-meter freestyle final was held at 3 PM. Ms. Deng Aodun of the Netherlands, the world record holder (1 minute 4.8 seconds), participated. It was generally expected that she could easily win the first place, but after the start, Ms. Mastenbroek of the Netherlands remained in the lead throughout the race, bravely moving forward, and reached the finish line first. Although the result was not as good as the world record, it broke the Games record of 1 minute 6.8 seconds set by Ms. Madison of the United States in the previous Games. Ms. Campbel of Argentina finished second, four meters behind. Ms. Arendt of Germany finished third by half an arm's length. The world record holder, Ms. Deng Aodun, finished fourth. The full results are as follows:

(1) Mastenbroek (Netherlands), 1 minute 5.9 seconds (New Games Record)

(2) Campbel (Argentina), 1 minute 6.4 seconds (New Games Record)

(3) Arendt (Germany), 1 minute 6.6 seconds (New Games Record)

(4) Deng Aodun (Netherlands), 1 minute 7.6 seconds

(5) Wagner (Netherlands), 1 minute 8.1 seconds

(6) McKean (USA), 1 minute 8.4 seconds

Men's 400-Meter Freestyle Preliminary Round. The men's 400-meter freestyle preliminary round was held at 3:15 PM, divided into six groups. The top two from each group and the best third-place finisher from each group participated in the semi-final. The results of each group, except for Uto Shunpei of Japan breaking the Games record (4 minutes 48.4 seconds set by Crabbe of the United States in the previous Games) in the fifth group, were not outstanding. The results are as follows:

First Group

(1) Kaneshiro Hiroshi (Japan), 4 minutes 52.6 seconds

Second Group

(1) Rivers (England), 4 minutes 57.2 seconds

(2) Proziwara (Germany), 5 minutes 11.7 seconds

(1) Makino Masazo (Japan), 4 minutes 51.5 seconds

(2) Flanagan (USA), 4 minutes 54.7 seconds

(1) Grove (Canada), 4 minutes 59.4 seconds

(2) Frisell (Germany), 5 minutes 3.1 seconds

On the 11th day of the Games, the schedule for the day is as follows: 7 AM: Calisthenics; 9 AM: Swimming, Fencing, Rowing; 2 PM: Rowing; 3 PM: Boxing, Calisthenics, Fencing, Basketball Game; 4 PM: Football (Austria vs. Poland); 4:30 PM: Hockey; 8:30 PM: Boxing. The swimming results are as follows:

Swimming

Men's 400-Meter Freestyle Semi-Final. The men's 400-meter freestyle semi-final was held at 10 AM, divided into two groups. In the first group, Japanese athlete Uto Shunpei finished first with a time of 4 minutes 48.4 seconds, tying the Games record, but the result was slower than in the preliminary round. In the second group, Japanese athlete Makino Masazo competed intensely with American Mediga, the world record holder (4 minutes 38.7 seconds). For the first 200 meters, Mediga was in the lead, about one meter ahead. After 200 meters, Makino Masazo accelerated and tried his best to catch up. When they reached the finish line, the two arrived at the same time, with no clear winner, and tied for first place, both breaking the Games record. The results of each group are as follows:

First Group

(1) Uto Shunpei (Japan), 4 minutes 48.4 seconds (Ties Games Record)

(3) Dalis (France), 4 minutes 55 seconds 7

The top four from each group participated in the semi-final. In the first group, Dutch athlete Ms. Sun Fu was agile and nimble, and took the lead by a five-meter margin. The result broke the record of 1 minute 18.3 seconds set by American Ms. Holm in the previous Games, and was also very close to the world record held by Holm (1 minute 16.2 seconds). Chinese athlete Ms. Yang Xiuqiong participated in the second group, and was about 20 meters behind the first place, ranking last. The results of each group are as follows:

Luan Cup Singles Semifinals: Sun and Hou Stalemate, Each Winning One Set, Match to Continue Today

The Luan Cup singles tennis tournament held by the Kangdi Club has progressed smoothly since its start. It has now reached the semifinal week. After Luo Qiren defeated Zai Shuzi in three sets of six to one the day before yesterday to win the final, the match between Hou Shangxiong and Sun Yaodong also started yesterday. Hou Shangxiong is one of the mainstays of the Kangdi Club. His tennis skills are sharp and agile. Sun Yaodong is known for his抽[chōu, a tennis technique] and is also good at volleying. He is also the highest contender for the championship. The two heroes met yesterday. Hou Shangxiong had a smooth first set, winning three games in a row. Unexpectedly, Sun Yaodong steadily pressed forward, surpassing him with a score of four to one. Then, each person's opening game was broken, resulting in a stalemate. In the end, Hou finally won the first set with a score of eight to six. The second set was even more intense. One game followed another, with alternating leads. The exciting waves made people unable to take their eyes off them. In the end, Sun Yaodong's long抽[chōu, a tennis technique] was successful, and several high-pressure shots were particularly impressive. He won the first set back with a score of eleven to nine. At this time, the autumn colors were evenly divided, and the atmosphere of the battle became even more tense. The third set was stalemated for a long time, with equal scores repeatedly. Until the sky was dark, it was still unresolved. After calculating the efforts, the score was still tied at five to five. Although they planned to continue and end this set, they were hindered by poor visibility. Therefore, both parties agreed to count each winning one set and disregard the five to five score in the third set. The match is scheduled to continue this afternoon to determine who will win the final. As for the final, which was originally scheduled to be held today, it is now too late and will have to be postponed. The date of the postponement has yet to be decided.

Standard Company Established Yesterday

Standard Sports Equipment Co., Ltd. held its inaugural meeting yesterday afternoon at the Shanghai United Society, Chóu Industry Building on Er Ma Road. Zhu Minyi, Xu Xiaochu, Sun Chóucheng, Chen Shenghai and other 126 households with 1,187 rights attended. Zhu Minyi was publicly elected as chairman, and Sun Chóucheng as recorder. When Zhu Zhongxi gave the opening speech, he elaborated on the relationship between sports equipment and national health. In the past, all sports equipment was purchased from abroad. Now, shares are being raised to establish a company and manufacture it ourselves, which can recover a lot of rights and interests. Then, Chen Yuze reported on the preparations. After accountant Wang Shuyu reported on the audit of the balance sheet and the amount of share funds received, six chapters and twenty-eight articles of the articles of association were passed. Then, directors and supervisors were elected by voting. Lu Jiayan, Shen Dazhong, Wang Qiusheng, Wang Renxian, and 4 gentlemen were elected. As a result of the voting, Zhu Minyi, Zhou Bangjun, Xu Zhiyi, Xia Xishi, Xu Duo, Lu Jiayan, Chen Zize and other seven gentlemen were elected as directors, and Wei Shaomang and Zhuang Xiaocai and other two gentlemen were elected as supervisors. After refreshments, everyone dispersed happily.

Education News

National Conditions of the Population in Northwest China: Central Government Subsidies for Compulsory Education Expenses. Shaanxi Has the Highest Population Density and the Most Enrolled Children.

Among the provinces in the Northwest region, including Shaanxi, Gansu, Qinghai, Xinjiang, Suiyuan, and Ningxia, Shaanxi has the highest population density. The Wei River and Han River basins have fertile land and a mild climate, so residents are concentrated there. In the northern areas of Yulin, Suide, Dingbian, and Baoan, the land is semi-desert and the climate changes drastically, so the population is sparse. The population density of Gansu is second to Shaanxi. Huixian County, Chengxian County in the southeast, and Gaolan in the west are the most densely populated areas. In the northwest, in Anxi, Dunhuang, and Yudu counties, sand accumulates and production is limited, so the population is relatively sparse. Near the Hetao area of Suiyuan, branch canals crisscross and the land is fertile, so the population is densely populated. The farther away from Hetao, the sparser the population becomes. Ningxia is located in the southeast of the Yellow River basin and belongs to the loess layer, which is suitable for cultivation, so residents mostly gather here. The Ruo River basin in the west is affected by groundwater, and plants also grow. People mostly live in tents along the coast. Apart from this, most areas are barren and sparsely populated. In Qinghai, the eastern areas of Xining and Huangyuan are densely populated. The northwest of Yushu is sandy and the climate is unpredictable, so residents are scattered. The southeast of Xinjiang is a desert area with few products and a very sparse population. The areas north and south of the Tianshan Mountains are relatively densely populated, followed by the southwest. In the entire northwest region, Xinjiang is probably the province with the sparsest population. The society has developed rapidly in recent years. Its publication, Children's Education, has recently greatly increased in sales, and the children's education series it has published has also won praise from elementary school teachers and parents in general.

Literacy Schools for Silk Factory Workers: Uniformly Start School Yesterday, a Total of 48 Factories with More Than 250 Classes, One Hour of Teaching Per Day for a Limited Period of Three Months

The teachers of the literacy classes for silk factory workers in Shanghai, after being registered and assigned by the Social Bureau, uniformly started school yesterday. The teaching time is from 5:00 PM to 6:00 PM every day, for a period of three months. Each factory has one school, and each school includes four to nine classes, with 50 students in each class. Each school has one head teacher. There are a total of 48 silk factories in the city, with more than 250 classes. The names of the factories are recorded as follows: Xinglun, Hengtai, Jiufeng, Tongyu, Xinchang, Yili, Guangyuan, Doutai, Xiangcheng, Liyuan, Yifeng, Changji, China, Baofu, Yuchang, Zhongyu, Fulunheng, Yongxing, Yiju, Zhenxiang, Dingchang, Yicheng, Shaodian, Qiaoyuan, Jiyu, Jiuyu, Meishuang, Dacheng, Fuchang, Dongxiang, Tailun, Xiexing, Yichangyong, Hongcha, Dafeng, Fuchang Factory, Hongchang, Gongda, Yutai, Qinyi, Yuanyu, Yuanji, Zhicheng, Yufeng, Family Life, Hengcang, Chengshuang, Yufeng.

Overview of Japanese Schools in Shanghai (3)

— Special Report from this Newspaper, Investigation by Hu Zuyin

5. Teaching Facilities

Based on the Imperial Rescript on Education of the Meiji Emperor of Japan, the educational policy of elementary schools is to develop a strong body for national life and to cultivate good and promising character, intelligence, and skills. The purpose of higher education for women is to improve women's general education, with particular emphasis on the cultivation of national morality and attention to the cultivation of feminine virtues. In implementation, solid and steady teaching policies for each subject are established, and at the same time, attention is paid to the development of children's minds and bodies, and a conscious learning attitude and ability are cultivated to seek the development and enrichment of knowledge and skills. The curriculum includes subjects such as ethics, reading, arithmetic, national history, geography, science, physical education, drawing, handicrafts, and music. Elementary school girls also have sewing, and elementary school English is an elective. Middle school girls also add cooking, housework, etiquette, education, and tea ceremony courses.

In terms of teaching, in addition to strictly following the detailed teaching guidelines, emphasis is also placed on regular field trips, which are carried out in the spring and autumn seasons of each school year according to the main points. Each month, when necessary, children can also be led on field trips. Children are also often led to observe school gardens and the vicinity of school buildings. At the same time, on scheduled dates, children are led to visit troops, barracks, warships, newspaper offices, factories, exhibitions, expositions, and other places.

Children's learning presentations can be held in the following events: (1) Academic and Arts Fair: A small meeting is held once each semester, and a large meeting is held at the end of each school year. Children can show the results of their usual learning at the meeting, so that they can encourage each other. (2) Exhibition: Held once a year to encourage children to work hard. (3) Concert: Held once a year to cultivate children's noble feelings. There are also educational films that are shown once a month to instill common sense of various subjects in children.

The school attaches great importance to children's preview and review work. Generally, first and second graders have about 30 minutes of preview and review time each day. Third and fourth graders have about one hour each day, and fifth and sixth graders have about one and a half hours of self-study time each day. In the reading room, many reference books, appreciation of various subjects, and children's reading materials are also prepared for children to study freely. Regarding the study of Chinese affairs, the school has separately compiled a supplementary reader for Japanese elementary school students in China to read.

Yarn and Cotton: Unwilling to Take in Stagnant Goods; This Month's Yarn Feels Even More Sluggish; Forward-Date Brokers Slightly Firmer in Taking Positions

The yarn market fell in the morning and rebounded at noon, but the trend this month remains sluggish. This is because there are many who have a lot of floating profits and are unwilling to take delivery, coupled with rumors that there are some stagnant goods, which are even less welcome, so the market situation is even more virtual, breaking through the 200 yuan mark. However, the situation for forward-date current yarn is good, and brokers are firm in pulling up prices. However, the overseas yarn and cotton market is gradually becoming flat and fatigued.

Near-Term Approaches the 200 Yuan Mark

In the morning opening of the traded yarn market, prices continued to decline for each month. This is because the delivery period for this month is approaching, with only two business days remaining. There are rumors that thousands of bales of arbitrage yarn must be delivered without a doubt. It is said that the sales of this type of traded yarn are very sluggish for a time. Therefore, the market condition this month is even more virtual, breaking through the 200 yuan mark. Forward-date yarn is dragged into the vortex, but some brokers, seeing that the stored yarn is less than before, are still inclined to be bullish. However, there are still over 26,000 bales of chips in the warehouse, and Yu Da (裕大), Tai Xing (泰興), Ming De (明德), Wang Tai Xing (望泰興), Da Chang Cheng (大昌成), Chang Feng (長豐), etc. have sold a lot. New Cotton Supply Gradually Increases; Traded Cotton Market Momentum Dampened; Rumors That Old Cotton in the Exchange Has Been Sold at Reduced Prices

The cotton market is calm, and the momentum is weakening. This is due to favorable weather conditions, which are of great benefit to cotton picking, coupled with the unfavorable trend of American cotton. Fortunately, the Indian cotton market is relatively expensive, and the listing of new cotton from various sources is gradually becoming abundant.

Far-Month Contracts Each Fall by About 10 Cents

However, although the bulls were active when the first lot opened, the momentum was still dampened. This is because the weather has been favorable recently, and new cotton is in the midst of an abundant flood, coupled with the unfavorable trend of American cotton, all months broke through the 12 cent mark. There is hope that the supply from various sources will gradually increase, and the market still lacks excitement. Sesame Exports Decrease Greatly in August

According to the report of the Shanghai Commodity Inspection Bureau of the Ministry of Industry, sesame exports in August totaled 6,281.60 metric tons, a sharp decrease of 41,169.26 metric tons compared with 47,450.86 metric tons in the same month last year. The total export volume in the first eight months of this year was 504,852.80 metric tons, which was also a decrease of 112,071.42 metric tons compared with the same period last year. As for the reason for its decline, it is generally due to the decrease in international consumption, the abnormal stagnation of European sales, and the quite sluggish situation in American markets. Although Japan and Italy have a strong desire to import, the overall calculation is still not as strong as last year. It is not optimistic about the export of sesame this year. The comparison of sesame export volume in August with the same month last year is listed on the left.

The sales of various goods in the market were sluggish, including broken japonica rice, thin paddy rice, new customer point rice, and old sheep point rice. The price of the new sheep point rice and Xinxin japonica rice was slightly reduced. The new port point rice was selected carefully for continued purchase. The market price of broken japonica rice and new port point rice was slightly higher by a few cents. The price of Xinxin japonica rice and sheep point rice was reduced by 200 to 300 cents. The price of Bai Yuan Dongxin japonica rice was flat.

New Sesame Selling Price Is Firm; Soybean Trend Is Also Stable

New sesame arrivals continue, and the Eastern Ocean gang continues to purchase. The retail market in this street and those who are gathering to make foreign goods are not weak in their desire to buy, so people are optimistic, and the goods owners are tightening up, resulting in sparse market transactions. It is estimated that more than 150 packages of Shashi sesame, 75 packages of Dangshan sesame, and 5 packages of Nanjing sesame were offered. The market price has not changed. The foreign merchants opened for trading, and 300 tons were opened on Saturday night, with the price being 11.9 yuan. Yesterday, there were 100 tons at 11.95 yuan, and then 12 yuan, but the transaction did not go through. The soybean trend is quite stable. The oil extraction plant is not slacking on its soybean demand because the price of soybean oil is on the rise and the cake market is stable. Yesterday, 1,200 to 1,300 packages of early yellow soybeans from Hankou, 200 packages of Qingjiangpu soybeans, and more than 100 packages of Yaowan soybeans were purchased. Other southern routes such as Fuzhou, Quanzhou, Shantou, Guangdong gang, and this street are all inquiring, and a total of 2,400 to 2,500 packages of various soybeans have been traded.

Piece Goods: Yarn and Thread Firmly Rise, Cotton Cloth Becomes More Popular; New Transactions in the Yangtze River and Henan and Shandong Are Booming; Hakka Merchants Need to Place Orders Early

Yesterday, the cotton cloth market was still good, and the demand for spot goods from various sources increased daily. Although the current trend of traded yarn and cotton is flat, the current yarn and thread are firm and scarce, resulting in an increasingly prosperous market for cotton cloth, white goods, and colored goods. Spot goods are greatly panicked, and Hakka merchants are placing orders in advance and waiting for distribution, otherwise it will be difficult to obtain them. Yesterday, Guangdong gang and other factories continued to purchase more than 300 pieces of thread tweed, fine cloth, fine twill, coarse cloth, straight tribute, and serge. Other southern routes, such as Yunnan and Fujian gangs, also had a strong desire to buy, and each traded more than 200 pieces. However, some replenishment goods are temporarily difficult to trade due to shortage and price increases. The new transactions of Sichuan and Tianjin gangs are rare, but the loading is still large. The new transactions and loading of floral flannel, white flannel, blue cloth, colored twill, thread tweed, floral plain straight tribute serge, and satin are all extremely prosperous along the Yangtze River and in Henan and Shandong inland. The market for each goods continues to be good. Xin Yu (新裕), Zhen Tai (振泰), Da Sheng (大生), Bao Xing (寳興) and other factories increased the price of heavy coarse cloth by 5 cents per piece, and the price of colored thread tweed also increased by 5 cents per code.

Sales of Woolen Fabrics Are All Smooth

Yesterday, the woolen fabric market was good, and the trend of each goods was brisk. The standard market was stable, and both zero and bulk transactions were prosperous. In addition to the best-selling products in this street, the mobilization and purchase from Tianjin, Qingdao, Beijing, Zhenjiang, Hangzhou, Ningbo and other places were also strong. The sales of straight tribute, serge, Walter tweed, Hailing tweed, Hailisi, Shi Pao Tuike Si (師泡推克四), Ping Hou tweed (平厚呢), yellow tweed, Melton, herringbone tweed, breeches tweed and other types were all extremely prosperous for a time. The wholesale price of China Wave Impact Master Pao Tuike Si (華波沖師泡推克四) for spot delivery was 6.6 yuan, the wholesale price of Mei Zui Shi Shun Feng De Li (美最時順風得利) was 6.5 yuan, the wholesale price of Rui Xing Huang Ni (瑞興黃呢) was 2.4 yuan, and the wholesale price of Bao Da (寳達) was 1.9 yuan.

Silk and Tea: The Autumn Cocoon Harvest in Jiangsu and Zhejiang Is Not Good; Silk Prices in This City Are Rising Very Quickly; However, the Transaction Has Stopped Due to the High Price

Yesterday, the silk market in this port was rising due to the poor harvest of autumn cocoons in Jiangsu and Zhejiang. Manufacturers are also holding on and unwilling to sell easily. It is learned that the cocoon price in Wuxi is between 27 and 28 yuan, while the price in Hangzhou is around 33 and 34 yuan. The other areas, such as Yixing, are roughly the same as Hangzhou. The manufacturer's asking price for the Shanghai white factory's Ching brand 202 grade raw silk has risen to 640 to 650 yuan. The price of Tian Tai Luo Bin Han (天臺羅濱漢) grade is 660 yuan, and the price of Feng Que Shuang Hu (蜂鵲雙虎) grade is about 670 yuan. The asking price for export silk delivery should be increased by about 15 yuan for foreign firm expenses before the transaction can be completed. Due to the rapid rise in prices, transactions have stalled. The foreign firm's silk market is even more deserted. Only a few sold yesterday from the user side. For example, the Zebra brand white factory's selling price was 667.5 yuan, which was an increase of 17.5 yuan compared to last week.

Precious Eyebrow Green Tea Sales Slightly

Yesterday, the foreign firm's green tea market situation was still quiet. Only the Tong Fu (同孚), Tian Xiang (天祥), Jin Long (錦隆), Yong Xing (永興) and other firms in the city bought precious eyebrow shrimp eye and other green teas, totaling more than 370 boxes. The selling price of precious eyebrows was 105 yuan, and the selling price of shrimp eyes was 53 yuan, which was unchanged from last week. The other needle eyebrow and show eyebrow goods are all trending flat. The Qimen black tea is still under negotiation yesterday. Judging from the current situation, the entire Wang Yu Tai (汪裕泰) is still promising.

According to the report of the Tea Industry Association, the green tea market is still quiet. The telegraphs for the previous week's selling of precious eyebrows and other products to foreign countries by various firms failed to get a response yesterday, Monday, so the transactions were extremely rare. However, Bai Tou's (白頭) purchase of Gong Xi (貢熙) was still active, with hundreds of boxes of transactions continuing. Tong Fu (同孚) and Xie He (協和) each purchased dozens of boxes of Tunxi and Suian (遂安) precious from extraction. The selling price was slightly worse than before. The big group of American firms had no transactions of Pingshui tea for a long time. Yesterday, Jin Long (錦隆) began to disassemble and handle five groups after receiving a call from the buyer, all of which were mid-to-lower grade pearl teas. The selling price was still similar to before. The market situation was slightly more active than last week.

Sugar Market: 10,000+ bags of Dutch coarse white arrive

Yesterday, the sugar market trend was stable and beautiful. The association's price for 24 coarse sand white was 21.55 yuan for spot goods and 6.6 yuan for transit goods. Dongbai 489 remained unchanged. The prices for local factory's refined white, Jinxin (金心), Dahua (大華), and No. 1 were all 20.5 yuan, and the rest were refunded. Guangchao (廣潮) gang offered more than 500 bags of Hainan red at 14 yuan, a rise of 10 to 20 cents. Huanggangqing (黃崗青) dozens of bags at 14.5 yuan, and Jian (建) gang offered 700+ bags of Diaoqing (刁青) at 13 yuan, a rise of 20 cents. 16,452 bags of Dutch coarse white, Shanzhisha (山芝沙), and Danny (丹尼) were imported and transported in.

The cooperative company held its first tender for Guangdong coarse white of the week yesterday, with a total quota of more than 9,000 bags. The bidding price was as before. 1,480 bags of Shunde factory's Five Rams (五羊) coarse white, and another 10 bags from Quxi factory were sold at 21 yuan. Another 1,000 bags from the Shixin factory were sold at 21.2 yuan, and another 205 bags of medium sand white were sold at 19.3 yuan.

Hardware: Belgian Factory Strike; White Lead Sheets Increase in Price Frequently

The price of white lead sheets has been rising in recent overseas telegrams. According to investigation, the reason is actually due to the strike in the Belgian factory. The most arrivals of white lead sheets in this port are Belgian goods. Although Germany, Poland, and other countries also have arrivals, the number is very small, so Belgian goods are the most popular in the market. Recently, due to the fact that Belgian orders must be changed to be shipped three months later, it is inevitable that the inventory in Shanghai will be out of stock in the future. The standard has risen sharply. The current market transaction is also more than before. The factory side is deeply afraid that there will be a shortage of goods in the future. It was found that a total of four or five hundred bundles were sold in the past two days, and the market price has increased by two to three yuan compared to before. For example, No. 2 is sold at 152 yuan per bundle, No. 3 at 140 yuan, Nos. 4 and 5 at 130 yuan, Nos. 6 and 7 at 127 yuan, and Nos. 8 and above are sold at 125 to 128 yuan. According to the recent observation of market sentiment, it is feared that the market price will not be easy to loosen for a while.

Statistics: Overview of Tung Oil Export and Output in August: Exports Decrease Sharply - Domestic Sales Are Booming

According to the report of the Shanghai Commodity Inspection Bureau of the Ministry of Industry, tung oil exports in August totaled 3,128.56 metric tons, a decrease of 4,590 metric tons compared with 7,719.04 metric tons in the same month last year. The total for the first eight months of this year also decreased by more than 25,000 metric tons compared with the same period last year. It can be seen that tung oil exports this year are declining day by day, and there is a tendency to get worse. The sluggish sales in the UK and the US have almost led to this.

Domestic sales of tung oil this year, on the other hand, have shown progress. For example, the efforts of Qingdao, Yantai, Tianjin and other groups have been unusually active. Therefore, compared to the total number of exports from Shanghai to various ports in the first eight months of this year with the same period last year, it has increased by 5,000 metric tons, almost doubling the total number compared to the same period last year, an increase of about 5,000 metric tons, almost doubling the giant. The booming output in August shows that the future is promising. The quantity of tung oil for export and domestic sales in August is listed in two tables below.
